GT Equivalence Verification (BPG6)
============================================================
GT: -c0*c1*P + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fully concrete) depends **only on P** and has the structure
\[
(-6.2168\cdot 1.41275)P + 0.85788(1-P/79.2026)P + 0.85788\,P^{1/3}+0.85788\,P.
\]
So GT is a sum of **(i)** a linear term in \(P\), **(ii)** a quadratic term in \(P\) (from \(-(0.85788/79.2026)P^2\)), and **(iii)** a fractional power term \(P^{1/3}\). There is **no \(t\)** dependence, no logs/exp/tanh/sin/Max/Abs, and no rational-in-\(P\) denominators.

A candidate can match only if we can (a) eliminate all \(t\)-dependence for all \(t\), and (b) reduce the \(P\)-dependence to exactly a linear + quadratic + \(P^{1/3}\) combination (with correct coefficients achievable by choosing constants).

---

### 1. \(P\cdot P^{c0}c1 + Pc2 + c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 e^{c6 t}/t^5 + c7 e^{c8 t}\log(Pc9+1)\)
Has unavoidable \(t\)-terms unless their coefficients are 0: set \(c3=c5=c7=0\) removes them. Then left with \(c1 P^{c0+1}+c2P\). No way to produce both a \(P^2\) term and a \(P^{1/3}\) term simultaneously (only one power term). Not match.

### 2. \(c0P^2 + c1\tanh(c2 t+c3)+ c4\log(c5 e^{P^{c6}c7}+1)\)
To remove \(t\): need \(c1=0\) (or impossible identity). Then log term is \(\log(c5 e^{(\cdot)}+1)\), not a pure power \(P^{1/3}\) and cannot become polynomial+fractional power for all \(P\). Not match.

### 3. \(c0P^3 + c1P^2 + c2P^2 + Pc3 e^{c4 t}+Pc5 + c7 P^{c6}/(Pc8+1)+c9\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Remove constant: set \(c9=0\). Still has \(P^3\) unless \(c0=0\). Then has \(P^2\) and \(P\) plus a rational term \(P^{c6}/(Pc8+1)\). To become \(P^{1/3}\) youŌĆÖd need \(c8=0\) so denominator constant 1, giving \(c7P^{c6}\). Then you can set \(c6=1/3\). Now expression is \( (\text{some})P^2+(\text{some})P + (\text{some})P^{1/3}\). This *looks promising*, but note GTŌĆÖs quadratic coefficient is fixed negative \(-0.85788/79.2026\) and linear coefficient is a specific value; candidate can set \(c1+c2\) to that quadratic coefficient and \(c5\) to the linear coefficient. Yes, this candidate **can** match GT by:
- \(c3=0,\ c4\) arbitrary
- \(c9=0\)
- \(c0=0\)
- \(c8=0\)
- \(c6=1/3\)
- choose \(c7=0.8578822735168387\)
- choose \(c1+c2 = -0.8578822735168387/79.20259671838578\)
- choose \(c5 =\) (GT linear coefficient total)
But check GT linear coefficient: GT has three linear contributions: \(-6.2168\cdot1.41275 P + 0.85788\cdot 1\cdot P + 0.85788 P\). That is \((-6.2168\cdot1.41275 + 0.85788 + 0.85788)P\). Candidate has only \(Pc5\) as linear term (since we set \(c3=0\)). So set \(c5\) equal to that total. Therefore **candidate 3 matches**.

### 4. \(Pc0\log(1+c1/P)+Pc2+Pc3\log(1+c4/P)+c5+c6\tanh(\cdot)\)
To remove \(t\): set \(c6=0\). Remove constant: set \(c5=0\). Still has \(P\log(1+\alpha/P)\) terms, which are not algebraic powers; cannot equal a combination of \(P, P^2, P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\). Not match.

### 5. \(Pc0 + P^{c1}c2 t^2/(c3+t^2)+ P^{c1}c4/(c3+t^2)+ P^{c5}c6 + \text{(terms with }1/(c3+t^2))\)
To remove \(t\)-dependence for all \(t\), must zero out every term with \((c3+t^2)\) denominators: set \(c2=c4=c7=c8=c9=0\). Then left with \(Pc0 + c6 P^{c5}\). Only one power besides linear; cannot produce both \(P^2\) and \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

### 6. \(c0P^2 + c1P + c3P^{c2} + c4 t/(c5+c6 e^{c7 t})\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c4=0\). Then we have \(c0P^2 + c1P + c3P^{c2}\). Choose \(c2=1/3\) and \(c3=0.85788\), and set \(c0\) and \(c1\) to GTŌĆÖs quadratic and linear coefficients. This matches GT exactly. (So 6 matches as well.)

### 7. \(c0P^2 + c1P^2/(P+c2)+Pc3+Pc4 e^{c5 t}+ c6 t/(c7+c8 e^{c9 t})\)
Remove \(t\): need \(c4=0\) and \(c6=0\). Then has \(P^2/(P+c2)\) which is rational, not a pure power; cannot become \(P^{1/3}\) and also keep polynomial terms for all \(P\). Not match.

### 8. \(c0P^2 + c1P^2 + Pc2 + Pc3 + c4 e^{c5 t} + c6 e^{c7 t}/t^5 + c8\)
To remove \(t\): set \(c4=c6=0\). Remove constant: set \(c8=0\). Left with only \(P^2\) and \(P\) terms, no \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

### 9. \(Pc0 + c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4 t}/t^5 + c5\)
Even if \(t\)-terms removed by \(c1=c3=0\) and constant by \(c5=0\), left only linear \(P\). Missing \(P^2\) and \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

### 10. \(c0P^2 + c1 e^{c2 t} + c3 e^{c4 t}/t^5 + c5\)
After removing \(t\)-terms and constant, only \(P^2\). Missing linear and \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

### 11. \(c0P^2+c1P^2+c2P^2 e^{c3 t}+Pc4+Pc5+c6 e^{c7 t}+c8 e^{c9 t}/t^5\)
Remove \(t\): must set \(c2=c6=c8=0\). Then only \(P^2\) and \(P\). Missing \(P^{1/3}\). Not match.

### 12. \(c0P^2 + c1P + c2P(Pc3+1)^{c4} + c5 e^{c6 t} + c7 e^{c8 t}/t^5\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c5=c7=0\). The term \(P(Pc3+1)^{c4}\) cannot equal \(P^{1/3}\) for all \(P\) (itŌĆÖs affine-in-\(P\) inside a power). If \(c3=0\) it becomes \(P\) (not \(P^{1/3}\)); if \(c4=0\) it becomes \(P\). Not match.
